<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于Transformer的神经算子方法通常假设固定的计算域大小，导致其在面对推理时比训练时更大的空间域时泛化能力不足。本文旨在解决这一局限性，实现零样本（Zero-shot）下的域扩展推理。

Method: 提出了一种在注意力逻辑（Attention Logits）计算中引入可分解偏置（Decomposable Bias）的方法，以实现空间局部性；结合旋转位置嵌入（Rotary Positional Embeddings），在保持模型结构兼容性的同时，赋予模型可控的空间支持能力，使其能够处理远超训练域规模的推理任务。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在两个偏微分方程基准测试以及一个三维工业大气流应用中，显著提升了模型在更大空间域上的零样本泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于可分解偏置和旋转位置编码的Transformer架构，成功实现了在不改变模型结构的前提下，对偏微分方程求解器进行空间域扩展（Domain Extension），证明了空间局部性和平移等变性对于零样本推理泛化能力的决定性作用。

Abstract: Transformer-based neural operators have shown remarkable performance for approximating solution operators of partial differential equations on complex geometries. However, existing approaches implicitly assume a fixed domain size, which limits their ability to generalize at inference. In this work, we investigate domain extension, namely zero-shot inference on spatial domains that are significantly larger than those encountered during training. We argue that this setting fundamentally requires spatial locality and translation equivariance. We propose to implement this locality via a decomposable bias in the attention logits computation, enabling finely controllable locality while remaining fully decomposable into query-key inner products and directly compatible with optimized attention kernels. Combined with rotary positional embeddings, it enables expressive embeddings with controllable spatial support without altering the transformer architecture. We empirically show that our approach substantially improves zero-shot generalization to larger domains across two PDE benchmarks and a 3D industrial atmospheric flow application. Our code and datasets are available at https://github.com/cerea-daml/domain-extension.

### [164] [Realizing Native INT8 Compute for Diffusion Transformers on Consumer GPUs: A Fused INT8 GEMM Kernel for Ideogram 4.0](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14598)
*Ali Asaria,Tony Salomone,Deep Gandhi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对消费级Ampere GPU上INT8推理性能低下的问题，本文通过构建定制化的融合Triton内核，绕过了低效的反量化路径，实现了INT8推理的显著加速，使其在RTX 3090上超越了FP8和NF4方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散Transformer的INT8量化在消费级Ampere GPU上并未带来预期速度提升，反而因为软件实现层面的反量化开销，导致其推理速度慢于FP8和NF4，未能发挥INT8硬件张量核心的性能优势。

Method: 研究人员识别出当前INT8实现因反量化至BF16而导致无法利用硬件加速的性能瓶颈。为此，他们开发了一个单一融合的Triton INT8 GEMM内核，直接利用Ampere张量核心进行INT8矩阵乘法（int8xint8->int32），同时在核函数结尾融合了按标记和通道的反量化操作及偏置项。

Result: 该方法在单张RTX 3090显卡上，使INT8 GEMM层的运行速度提升了2.8-4.2倍。端到端推理时，768px分辨率下获得约1.1倍的加速，1024px分辨率下推理时间缩短至156.5秒，优于同机型下的NF4（164.5秒）和FP8（172.9秒）基准，且图像质量指标保持一致。

Conclusion: 在消费级Ampere架构GPU（如RTX 3090）上，通过深度定制的Triton INT8 GEMM内核，可以有效挖掘硬件INT8张量核心的计算能力，使INT8量化成为扩散Transformer推理最快的方案。然而，该优势具有硬件特定性，在A100或B200等更高级架构上，原生支持的高性能BF16/FP8路径依然更优。

Abstract: Post-training INT8 (W8A8) quantization of diffusion transformers is widely deployed as a speed optimization, yet on consumer Ampere GPUs it is frequently slower than the FP8 and NF4 alternatives it is meant to beat. We trace this to a software artifact: the production "INT8" forward quantizes weights and activations only to immediately dequantize them back to bf16 and run a bf16 matrix multiply, never engaging the GPU's INT8 tensor cores, so the hardware's compute advantage is left entirely unrealized. We close this gap with a single fused Triton INT8 GEMM (int8xint8->int32 on Ampere tensor cores, with per-token x per-channel dequantization and bias folded into the epilogue, autotuned per GEMM shape) dropped into the Ideogram 4.0 diffusion transformer's linear layers in place of the dequantize-to-bf16 path. In the kernel, the int8xint8->int32 accumulation is bit-exact against torch._int_mm and the dequantized output matches the reference at cosine similarity 1.0 with no NaNs, running 2.8-4.2x faster than bf16 per GEMM. End to end it delivers a ~1.1x (~9-10%) speedup at 768px, and at 1024px it generates an image in 156.5 s on a single RTX 3090, faster than the single-card NF4 (164.5 s) and FP8 (172.9 s) baselines, at no measurable quality cost on these point estimates (PickScore/CLIPScore). INT8 thus goes from the slowest variant to the fastest, and 1024px becomes single-GPU feasible. The primary speed criterion (beat FP8, by ~9.5%) is comfortably met; the NF4 margin (~4.9%, single-run n=4) is within run-to-run variance we did not quantify and is best read as consistent with meeting the stretch target. We close with an honest deployment map: the win is specific to consumer Ampere, and on A100 and B200 the same kernel loses to those cards' fast native bf16/FP8 paths.

</details>


### [165] [A Statistical and Machine Learning Framework for Operational Threshold Detection and Deployable Dispatch Controller Development in Hydrogen Multi-Energy Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14601)
*Shadi Heenatigala,Hasanika Samarasinghe*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢能多能源系统（H-MES）的运行受多种不确定因素（如可再生能源波动、电力需求）的影响，传统的建模方法往往难以兼顾解释性与预测的准确性。本研究旨在通过分析一年期高分辨率运行数据，探究不同输入变量对系统运行的影响机制，并评估统计与机器学习方法在描述及优化此类复杂系统中的有效性。

Abstract: This study presents a statistical and machine learning framework for characterizing a hydrogen-based multi-energy system (H-MES) using one year of high-resolution operational data. Statistical analysis revealed a binary operation driven by renewable surplus, with solar irradiance explaining 45.7% of rank-based variance in hydrogen production, a large effect by conventional standards. Only high-irradiance periods triggered meaningful electrolyzer engagement, while electricity demand exerted a weaker inverse suppression effect ($ε^2 = 0.126$). Multiple regression confirmed electrolyzer power as the dominant linear predictor, with a synergistic solar-wind interaction. Notably, Random Forest analysis ranked wind output first in predictive importance despite its weak bivariate correlation (r = 0.167), revealing non-linear dynamics invisible to parametric methods. A sequence model exploited strong 24-hour autocorrelation (r = 0.845) for operational forecasting, while a reinforcement learning agent optimized hydrogen revenue dispatch. The core contribution is demonstrating that statistical and machine learning approaches are complementary for H-MES modeling and control.

### [166] [Neither Parallel Nor Sequential: How DiffusionGemma Actually Commits Tokens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14620)
*Ali Asaria,Tony Salomone,Deep Gandhi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文通过对DiffusionGemma 26B进行深度监控，揭示了扩散语言模型的解码过程并非真正意义上的并行，其Token提交顺序表现为随观察粒度变化的动态特性，并指出模型“块大小”本质上是测量手段产生的伪影，而非架构本身的固有属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管扩散语言模型被宣传为并行、非自回归的解码器，但其真实的Token提交顺序往往缺乏实证研究。作者旨在探究这些模型在实际生成过程中，Token的提交顺序究竟是如何决定的，以及所谓的“块大小”等特性是否真正反映了模型架构的本质。

Method: 研究人员对DiffusionGemma 26B模型进行了仪器化（instrumentation）改造，通过钩取其采样器的接受步骤（accept step），实时记录各个位置token提交的时间、顺序及置信度。实验涵盖了686个提示词和六种不同的任务机制，并针对评估中的混淆因素（如EOS填充、批处理平局、提交非单调性等）开发了一套严谨的测量分析框架。

Result: 研究发现：1. 模型的解码过程既非完全并行，也非严格的块自回归；2. Token的提交顺序随着观察粒度的粗化而逐渐增强；3. 模型倾向于在大规模同步批次中提交Token，批次内部顺序往往是未定义的；4. 提交顺序与任务类型高度相关（如JSON生成顺序随意），且提交置信度在数学推理中与正确率相关，但在事实回忆任务中无意义。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，扩散语言模型的解码过程并非传统定义的“并行”或“块自回归”，其表现出的顺序特征高度依赖于测量粒度。模型在生成过程中存在一种随观察尺度平滑变化的偏向性，且在不同任务类型（如结构化JSON与数学推理）中呈现出差异化的提交行为。此外，该论文强调了在评估解码顺序时必须考虑到提交非单调性、批次连接及填充干扰等方法论因素。

Abstract: Open diffusion language models are marketed as parallel, non-autoregressive decoders, yet the order in which a shipped checkpoint actually commits its tokens is almost never measured. We instrument DiffusionGemma 26B, a masked discrete-diffusion mixture-of-experts model built on Gemma 4, hooking its sampler's accept step to record which canvas positions commit, when, and at what confidence. Across a 686-prompt, six-regime probe suite we find that its decoding is neither parallel nor block-autoregressive: it follows a partial left-to-right commit bias whose apparent strength depends almost entirely on the granularity at which you look. Order is weak token by token and strengthens smoothly as the analysis is coarsened, so the model's "block size" turns out to be an artifact of the measuring ruler rather than the architecture. The model commits in large simultaneous batches, leaving much of the within-batch order genuinely undefined rather than merely unobserved. The behaviour is regime-dependent: structured JSON is committed in essentially arbitrary order, and a position's commit confidence tracks correctness on mathematical reasoning but carries no signal on factual recall. Commitment is aggressive, finishing in a short late burst well inside the step budget, while task accuracy matches the model's autoregressive Gemma-4 sibling. Beyond these findings, our central contribution is methodological: measuring decoding order honestly demands handling trailing-EOS padding, within-regime confounding, commit non-monotonicity, block-size sensitivity, and large commit-batch ties, each of which can otherwise manufacture a decoding-order result that is not really there.

### [167] [Graph Diffusion Residuals for Control-Function Instrumental Variables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14636)
*Rui Wu,Zongyuan Chen,Hong Xie,Defu Lian,Enhong Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为A-IHF的新型控制函数估计方法，通过图扩散技术解决了高容量模型中残差信息被过度拟合的问题，在因果估计任务中展现出卓越的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 控制函数工具变量估计器依赖于第一阶段残差，而非单纯的预测值。在高容量模型中，第一阶段往往会过度拟合（插值）处理变量，导致残差项包含的信息量不足，进而影响因果推断的准确性。

Method: 提出自适应各向异性工具热流（A-IHF）方法。该方法将处理变量视为图特征上的信号，通过先导扩散检测处理变量的跳变，衰减跳变处的导电性，并利用稀疏图预解式计算控制函数，同时结合图广义交叉验证和图可采纳性过滤进行观测选择。

Result: 在54个合成基准测试中，A-IHF在平均结构响应均方误差（MSE）方面表现最优，并在32个测试场景中显著优于其他核、树、Boosting及神经网络等基准模型，特别是在捕捉到分段平滑结构时表现尤为突出。

Conclusion: A-IHF 通过在图结构上进行各向异性扩散，成功解决高维第一阶段模型中因过度拟合导致的控制函数残差信息丢失问题，在处理复杂选择偏差方面优于现有的多种非参数方法。

Abstract: Control-function instrumental variable estimators need a first-stage residual, not merely a first-stage prediction. High-capacity first stages can interpolate treatment and leave too little residual information for the outcome equation. We study Adaptive Anisotropic Instrumental Heat Flow (A-IHF), a deterministic graph-diffusion residual extractor for flexible control functions. A-IHF treats treatment as a signal on a graph of first-stage features, uses pilot diffusion to detect large treatment jumps, attenuates conductance across those jumps, and computes the generated control with a sparse graph resolvent. Its observational selection rule uses only $(Z,X)$, combining graph generalized cross-validation, roughness, residualized-treatment relevance, and graph-admissibility filtering. The analysis decomposes error into structural leakage, residual attenuation, and residualized treatment variation, yielding finite-sample bounds, graph-admissibility rates under latent piecewise-smooth geometry, and finite-path selection calibration. Across 54 synthetic benchmark cells with tuned graph, kernel, tree, boosting, series, and neural control-function baselines, guarded observational A-IHF has the lowest average structural-response MSE; the A-IHF family beats the best non-A-IHF baseline in 32 cells. Performance is strongest when the graph captures piecewise-smooth first-stage structure.

### [168] [Online Convex Optimization with Sublinear Noisy Probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14640)
*Simone Di Gregorio,Anupam Gupta,Stefano Leonardi,Matteo Russo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了带有限且带噪成对探测预算的在线凸优化问题，证明了通过有限的探测反馈可以实现遗憾的显著缩减，并给出了在多种参数下均达到最优的遗憾界分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的在线凸优化（OCO）研究通常假设完全反馈或仅限于特定场景。研究者希望在更一般化的框架下，探讨当预算有限且反馈带有噪声的情况下，成对比较（pairwise probing）如何帮助降低累积遗憾（regret），并弥合专家设置与连续决策空间之间的鸿沟。

Method: 本文引入了一个统一的探测模型，涵盖了专家设置中的次线性查询和OCO中的成对比较反馈。作者使用了基于二阶（方差）分析的连续指数权重（Continuous Exponential Weights）算法，通过量化探测带来的方差缩减效应，推导出了遗憾界，并分析了噪声参数δ对性能的影响。

Result: 在$k$次$\delta$-噪声成对探测下，获得的遗憾界为$O\left(\min\left\{\sqrt{dT\ln T},\; \frac{dT\ln T}{k|1-2\delta|}\right\}\right)$。该结果在$T$、$k$和$\delta$上几乎是最优的（仅差对数因子）。对于有限决策集（专家设置），该结果在所有参数（包括维度$d$）上均达到了紧致性。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一个统一的在线凸优化（OCO）探测模型，证明了即使是次线性的带噪成对探测预算，也足以显著改善最坏情况下的遗憾界。该方法通过方差缩减效应和二阶指数权重算法，实现了在探测预算、维度、噪声参数和总轮数之间的最优平衡。

Abstract: We study Online Convex Optimization (OCO) over a convex set $K\subseteq \mathbb R^d$, where in each round $t$ the learner selects $x_t\in K$ and then observes a convex loss $f_t:K\to[0,1]$, with the goal of minimizing regret to the best fixed decision in hindsight. We introduce a unified probing model that generalizes two recent lines of work: sublinear best-expert queries in the experts setting, and pairwise (comparison-based) feedback available every round in OCO. In our framework, the learner has a budget of $k\le T$ pairwise probes; on a probed round it may query two points and learn which one has smaller loss.
  Our main result shows that even a sublinear and noisy probe budget can provably improve worst-case regret in the full feedback OCO regime. With $k$ $δ$-noisy pairwise probes, we obtain: $ \text{Reg}_T \le O\left(\min\left\{\sqrt{dT\ln T},\; \frac{dT\ln T}{k|1-2δ|}\right\}\right) $, which is tight (up to logarithmic factors in $T$) across $T$, $k$ and $δ$. Specifically regarding the noise parameter $δ\in [0,1]$, the regret guarantee smoothly degrades as the oracle response approaches a coin flip, i.e., $δ$ is close to $\frac{1}{2}$. When applying the same techniques to a finite $K$ for the prediction with $d$ experts setting, the resulting rates are instead completely tight in all parameters, including $d$.
  Our analysis gives a streamlined treatment of pairwise probing in OCO by quantifying the benefit of probing via a variance reduction effect, combined with a second-order (variance-based) analysis of Continuous Exponential Weights.

</details>


### [169] [Which Directions Matter? Sparse Design for Affine Robust Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14648)
*Pedro Chumpitaz-Flores,My Duong,Juan S. Borrero,Kaixun Hua*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在鲁棒机器学习中如何从有限字典中选择最优的不确定性方向。通过将选择问题建模为具有次模性的覆盖问题，作者提出了一种高效的贪心选择算法，并提供了鲁棒性能的理论界限和校准规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器学习和优化领域，模型对不确定性模型的选择高度依赖。为了在面对有限字典和预算约束时，能够高效地确定鲁棒模型所需覆盖的不确定性方向，作者试图解决如何从预定义的集合中选择最优子集，以实现计算上的可追踪性和模型性能的鲁棒性。

Method: 1. 构建基于有限字典和预算约束的原子不确定性集；
2. 提出一种基于覆盖目标（涵盖梯度、对抗扰动或分布偏移）的数据驱动选择规则；
3. 利用次模函数优化理论，采用具有 (1-1/e) 近似保证的贪心算法进行子集选择；
4. 设计了用于评估损失的边界证书和样本外控制的半径校准方法。

Result: 文章提出了一种系统性的方法来选择不确定性集，使得仿射目标的鲁棒规划问题在计算上变得可解。该方法在理论上具有近似最优保证，并通过数据驱动的方式实现了对对抗扰动和分布偏移的有效防御。

Conclusion: 本文证明了所提出的覆盖目标函数具有单调性和次模性，通过贪心算法可以实现 (1-1/e) 的近似最优解。此外，文章提供的损失边界证明和半径校准规则，为鲁棒机器学习在实际应用中的性能控制提供了理论保证和实用工具。

Abstract: Robust machine learning and optimization rely on the uncertainty model choice. We investigate which uncertainty directions a model must cover when defined by a finite dictionary and a budget constraint. Selecting a subset forms an atomic uncertainty set with a closed form support function, yielding tractable robust programs for affine objectives. We propose a data driven selection rule based on a coverage objective over evaluation directions, including gradients, adversarial perturbations, or shifts observed on held out data. We prove this objective is monotone and submodular, supporting a greedy method with a $(1-1/e)$ approximation guarantee and a matching hardness barrier. We also provide a certificate bounding the loss from the selected subset and a radius calibration rule with out of sample control.

### [171] [Beyond task performance: Decoding bioacoustic embeddings with speech features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14662)
*Ines Nolasco,Jules Cauzinille,Marius Miron,Gagan Narula,Milad Alizadeh,Emmanuel Fernandez,Matthieu Geist,Ellen Gilsenan-McMahon,Olivier Pietquin,Emmanuel Chemla,Sara Keen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了生物声学预训练模型在编码声学特征方面的有效性，发现模型间存在特征覆盖的互补性，并提出了一套基于声学特征可恢复性的模型选择指南。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前生物声学领域广泛使用预训练音频嵌入，但对于这些模型具体编码了哪些声学特征、哪些特征对特定任务有用尚不明确。这种“黑盒”特性阻碍了研究的透明度，并限制了模型在稀有物种或数据匮乏场景下的应用。

Method: 研究使用了88个eGeMAPS声学特征作为基准，涵盖了六个不同的生物分类群。通过应用线性与非线性回归探针（probes）来量化各类预训练模型对这些声学特征的编码能力，并结合归一化互信息（NMI）分析物种层面的特征显著性，从而评估模型表现。

Result: 研究发现：1. 没有任何单一模型能够完整覆盖所有的声学特征空间（“没有免费午餐”原则）；2. 将多个模型的嵌入拼接可获得最佳性能；3. 模型对响度（Loudness）特征的编码能力最强（R²=0.76），而对基频（F0）的恢复能力最弱（R²=0.33）。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，生物声学中的预训练模型在特征表示上存在互补性，不存在单一的最优模型。通过量化模型对特定声学特征的编码能力，研究为针对特定物种的生物声学任务提供了数据驱动的模型选择指南，有助于提高该领域研究的透明度和效率。

Abstract: Pretrained audio embeddings are standard in bioacoustics, yet little is known about which acoustic features these models encode, nor which are useful for a given task. This hinders transparency and limits extension to rare species or data-scarce domains. Here we reveal which speech-like features are encoded in bioacoustic representations. Using the 88~eGeMAPS features across six taxonomic groups, we apply linear and nonlinear regression probes to quantify which acoustic properties each model captures. Results confirm a ``no free lunch'' pattern: no single model captures the full feature space. A concatenated embedding achieves the highest performance, suggesting complementary acoustic space coverage across models. Loudness features are best encoded ($R^2 = 0.76$) while F0 is hardest to recover ($R^2 = 0.33$). By cross-referencing recoverability with per-species feature salience (NMI), we derive data-driven model selection guidance for bioacoustics.

### [172] [When to Write and When to Suppress: Route-Specialized Dual Adapters for Memory-Assisted Knowledge Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14668)
*Yining Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种基于路由机制的双适配器知识编辑方法，通过动态判断是否应用编辑记忆，成功实现了对模型知识的精确更新，同时有效抑制了对无关知识的副作用，在多个基准测试中表现卓越。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 知识编辑系统需要在更新特定事实的同时，保护相关但无关的知识不被破坏。现有的系统往往难以平衡事实更新与模型行为的稳定性，缺乏对“何时抑制编辑”这一核心问题的系统处理。

Method: 该研究提出了一个名为“Route-specialized Dual-adapter Editor”的系统。其核心是一个“相关性路由器”（Relevance Router），在推理时判断输入提示是否需要应用编辑记忆。如果是，则激活“编辑适配器”以更新事实；如果不是，则激活“局部性适配器”（Locality Adapter）以确保原始偏好不被错误修改。该方法通过分离编辑注入与抑制机制来优化性能。

Result: 在Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct和Qwen3-8B模型上，该方法在CounterFact、ZSRE和MQuAKE三个基准测试中均取得了最优的概率偏好准确率（例如在MQuAKE上达到0.9922）。消融实验证实，性能的提升主要归功于将编辑与抑制机制分离的设计，而非简单的LoRA参数增加。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种名为“路由化双适配器编辑”的方法，通过区分何时进行事实修改和何时保持原事实，有效解决了知识编辑中的干扰问题。实验证明，将编辑注入与非路径抑制相分离是提升编辑准确性和保持模型稳定性的关键。

Abstract: Knowledge editing systems must update selected facts while preserving nearby but irrelevant behavior. This paper studies this problem in a memory-assisted setting where an edit memory is retrieved at inference time and a parameter-efficient adapter corrects the model's object preference. We argue that the central design question is not only how to write an edit, but also when to suppress it. We introduce \method{}, a route-specialized dual-adapter editor. A relevance router first decides whether a prompt should receive an edit memory. Routed prompts use an edit adapter trained to prefer the new object over the original object; unrouted non-direct prompts use a separate locality adapter trained to preserve or restore the original-object preference. We evaluate \method{} on three 1,000-case protocols, \cf{}, \zsre{}, and \mquake{}, under the same memory protocol and two 7B/8B base models. On Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct, \method{} obtains the best overall probability-preference accuracy on all three benchmarks: 0.8180 on \cf{}, 0.8946 on \zsre{}, and 0.9922 on \mquake{}. The same trend holds on Qwen3-8B. Router ablations show that the relevant memory boundary differs across datasets: a lexical neural router is safest on \cf{}, while BGE embedding routing is better on \zsre{} and \mquake{}. Component and module ablations show that the gain mainly comes from separating edit injection from off-route suppression rather than from simply increasing LoRA capacity.

### [173] [Compressed Computation is (probably) not Computation in Superposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14673)
*Jai Bhagat,Sara Molas-Medina,Giorgi Giglemiani,Stefan Heimersheim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究指出“压缩计算”（CC）模型并非“叠加计算”的范例。其看似高效的计算能力实际上是由模型架构中意外引入的线性混合机制导致的，而非神经元层面的特征叠加。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨由Braun等人（2025）提出的“压缩计算”（CC）模型是否真正实现了“叠加计算”。该模型在仅有50个神经元的情况下计算100个ReLU函数且表现异常，作者旨在揭示这种现象背后的数学机制及其是否代表了预期的叠加计算能力。

Method: 通过将训练目标拆解为ReLU项和混合项进行对比分析；观察神经元方向在混合矩阵主成分子空间中的分布；构建基于混合矩阵的半非负矩阵分解（SNMF）基准模型，与原模型进行对比评估。

Result: 分析发现，CC模型的性能增益与混合矩阵的幅值直接相关；当移除该混合项时，性能优势消失。神经元方向集中在混合矩阵最大特征值对应的子空间中，证明模型受混合机制驱动而非特征叠加，现有的SNMF基准模型能部分重现其性能特征。

Conclusion: 该研究表明“压缩计算”（CC）模型并非“叠加计算”（Computation in Superposition）的有效玩具模型。其所谓的性能提升主要源于噪声残差流带来的意外混合矩阵，而非真正的特征叠加。

Abstract: We study whether the Compressed Computation (CC) toy model (Braun et al., 2025) is an instance of computation in superposition. The CC model appears to compute 100 ReLU functions with just 50 neurons, achieving a better loss than expected from only representing 50 ReLU functions. We show that the model mixes inputs via its noisy residual stream, corresponding to an unintended mixing matrix in the labels. Splitting the training objective into the ReLU term and the mixing term, we find that performance gains scale with the magnitude of the mixing matrix and vanish when the matrix is removed. The learned neuron directions concentrate in the subspace associated with the top 50 eigenvalues of the mixing matrix, suggesting that the mixing term governs the solution. Finally, a semi-non-negative matrix factorization (SNMF) baseline derived solely from the mixing matrix reproduces the qualitative loss profile and improves on prior baselines, though it does not match the trained model. These results suggest CC is not a suitable toy model of computation in superposition.

### [174] [Optimal Hidden-Target Learning for Online Inventory Optimization on General Convex Sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14679)
*Anthony Pineci,Yunzong Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了在线库存优化（OIO）的一种最优通用策略：通过将在线学习与一维队列控制相结合（范数对齐原理），解决了库存结转导致的复杂状态依赖问题，显著提升了在一般凸约束集下的遗憾控制能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线库存优化（OIO）的核心挑战在于库存结转（carryover）导致当前行动受过去状态制约。现有方法大多局限于简单的线性容量约束，缺乏针对一般凸约束集的通用最优策略。研究旨在解决如何在大规模、复杂的凸约束条件下实现最优的在线决策与遗憾控制。

Method: 作者提出了一种基于“范数对齐”（norm alignment）的分析框架，将库存优化问题简化为一维队列控制。具体方法是维护一个在线学习器选择的隐式目标，通过将该目标投影到当前的实时可行集来实现最优决策。该方法结合在线梯度下降作为基础学习器，实现了对一般凸约束集的适配。

Result: 研究证明了该方法对于任意有界凸容量集均达到最优，在一般凸集上的遗憾界从原来的反比提升至反平方根依赖（相对于通用需求概率）。此外，该方法首次实现了强凸损失下的多对数遗憾保证，并提供了首个能够适应欧几里得路径变化的动态遗憾保证。

Conclusion: 该研究通过“范数对齐”原理成功将复杂的在线库存优化问题简化为一维队列控制问题，不仅在理论上为一般凸约束集下的OIO提供了最优遗憾界，还通过实验验证了其在实际应用中的有效性。

Abstract: Online inventory optimization (OIO) is online convex optimization with physical memory: inventory carryover makes the feasible action set depend on the past. A natural principle, used in stochastic inventory learning and recently in OIO under a single linear capacity constraint, is to maintain a hidden target chosen by an online learner and implement its projection onto the currently feasible order-up-to set. We prove that this simple principle is optimal for OIO on arbitrary bounded convex capacity sets. With online gradient descent as the base learner, the method improves the best known regret guarantee for OIO on general convex sets from inverse to inverse-square-root dependence on the common-demand probability, and we prove a matching lower bound. The same principle gives the first polylogarithmic regret guarantee for strongly convex losses and the first dynamic regret guarantee adapting to Euclidean path variation on general convex capacity sets.
  The analysis introduces a norm alignment principle: the right state variable is the distance from the hidden target to the feasible set, measured in the same norm as the projection. Under norm alignment, this distance evolves pathwise as a scalar queue, with target movement as arrival and common demand as service. This reduction to one-dimensional queue control resolves the state dependence and extends the guarantees to general convex capacity sets, beyond the reach of prior productwise approaches. Experiments on synthetic and real-world inventory data corroborate the theory.

### [175] [A Complexity Measure for Active Learning in Multi-group Mean Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14690)
*Abdellah Aznag,Rachel Cummings,Adam N. Elmachtoub*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了多组均值估计中的主动学习问题，首次推导了最小化最坏情况不确定性的通用下界，量化了预算、数据异构性和模型复杂度（VLC）对学习难度的影响，并验证了现有算法在处理极端异构数据时的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决多组均值估计中主动学习的最优采样策略问题，特别是如何优化预算分配以最小化各组间最坏情况下的不确定性指标，并填补该目标函数缺乏通用下界理论的空白。

Method: 提出了局部极小极大（local minimax）框架，通过构建损失诱导的l1几何空间和基于表示的实例生成器（将硬实例构造简化为随机矩阵计算），推导了针对有限方差假设类的首个通用下界。

Result: 证明了包含预算项、异方差指数和模型依赖复杂度（VLC）的通用下界。通过对比发现，该理论在广泛范围内接近最优（相差对数因子），并指出了现有算法在高度异构场景下的性能缺陷。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了多组均值估计中最大风险目标的主动学习极限，通过引入方差局部曲率（VLC）量化了模型复杂性，并证明了现有算法在处理高度异构实例时存在系统性差距，为该领域的下界理论提供了严谨的数学框架。

Abstract: We study a \emph{max-risk} objective for active learning in a multi-group mean estimation $d$-armed bandits: a learner adaptively allocates a budget of $T$ samples across $d$ groups to minimize the worst-case uncertainty index $\max_{k\in[d]}σ_k^2/n_k$, where $σ_k$ is the standard deviation of the distribution of arm $d$, and $n_k$ is the number of times arm $d$ is sampled. We develop a local minimax framework and prove the first general lower bound for this objective, valid for any finite-variance hypothesis class. The bound separates difficulty into three orthogonal factors: a \emph{budget} term, a \emph{heteroscedasticity} index measuring how unevenly the uncertainty is spread across arms, and a model-dependent complexity measure, the \emph{Variance Local Curvature} ($\mathrm{VLC}$), which captures how much information a local change of variance creates inside the hypothesis class. For smooth classes, the $\mathrm{VLC}$ is a reparametrization of a variance--Fisher information, with closed-form values for common families. Benchmarking against the strongest available upper bound shows near-optimality up to logarithmic factors in broad regimes, and pinpoints a systematic gap in highly heterogeneous instances. Our proof introduces two key ingredients: a loss-induced $\ell_1$ geometry on the decision space, and a representation-based instance generator that reduces hard-instance construction to an explicit random matrix calculation.

</details>

### [176] [Personalization and Evaluation of Conversational Information Access](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13717)
*Hideaki Joko*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文针对对话式信息访问（CIA）系统，提出了一套包含个人上下文提取（CREL）、个性化回复生成（LAPS）以及系统性能评估（FACE）的完整解决方案，旨在构建更准确、更懂用户的对话检索系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着用户倾向于从传统的链接列表转向直接的对话式回复，现有的信息检索系统面临着整合个人上下文以提供个性化、可靠服务的挑战。该论文旨在解决对话式信息访问（CIA）中上下文提取困难、个性化回复生成复杂以及系统评估缺乏解释性与有效性这三个关键问题。

Method: 1. 上下文提取：通过定义对话中的实体链接（EL）任务，构建了ConEL数据集，并提出了针对对话场景的CREL方法；2. 个性化生成：提出了LAPS方法，用于高效构建大规模人类编写的个性化对话数据集，并研究了如何利用用户偏好生成个性化回复；3. 系统评估：提出了一种名为FACE的自动、无需参考的评估方法，用于对完整对话进行评价，并确保其结果与人类判断高度一致。

Result: 研究证明了提出的CREL方法能有效提取对话实体，LAPS方法成功降低了构建个性化数据集的成本，且FACE评估指标在对话系统质量评估中展现出与人类判断的高度相关性，显著提升了CIA系统的可解释性与交互体验。

Conclusion: 该研究通过从上下文提取、个性化生成到系统评估的全链路探索，为构建更可靠、更具个性化的对话式信息访问（CIA）系统提供了理论基础与实践方法，强调了系统评价的解释性与人类偏好对齐的重要性。

Abstract: Conversational interactions have reshaped information retrieval systems, as users increasingly favour direct answers over traditional hyperlinks. To build reliable Conversational Information Access (CIA) systems that account for personal context, this thesis addresses challenges: (1) personal context extraction, (2) personalized response generation, and (3) effective and interpretable system evaluation. First, we tackle personal context extraction by studying what Entity Linking (EL) in conversations entails, introducing a dataset for conversational entity linking (ConEL), and proposing CREL, a novel EL method tailored for conversational settings. Second, we focus on personalized response generation by proposing LAPS, a method for efficiently constructing large-scale, human-written, personalized conversational datasets, and using them to study how users' preferences can be utilized to generate personalized responses. Finally, we address the need for effective and interpretable system evaluation by introducing FACE, an automatic, reference-free method that assesses entire conversations and aligns closely with human judgments.

</details>


### [177] [Nomenclature Ontology for Medical And Disease names (NOMAD): taxonomy of types and origins of disease names](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13719)
*Spiros Denaxas,Cai Ytsma,Giannos Louloudis,Jackie MacArthur,Harry Hemingway*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了疾病命名本体论（NOMAD），首次对ICD-10-CM中的两万余种疾病名称进行了系统化的命名习惯分类，揭示了医学术语背后的结构化特征、学科差异及社会文化偏见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类疾病命名法在过去几个世纪中呈有机增长，使用了多种语言且缺乏统一框架，导致命名方式极其多样且存在异质性。因此，研究旨在构建一个系统化的框架来描述和分析这些命名习惯。

Method: 研究人员开发了名为NOMAD的元分类法（Meta-taxonomy），包含9个顶层类别和20个子类别。通过三阶段机器学习流水线，对ICD-10-CM 2026索引中的22,548个疾病术语进行了多标签分类。同时，通过对10%的样本进行人工核查来评估分类准确性。

Result: 分类覆盖了99.1%的术语，平均每个词条有2.12个标签。结果显示：解剖学分类最为普遍（63.8%）；命名中的性别偏见明显，仅2.6%的命名源自女性；不同医学分支表现出显著的认识论差异（如感染性疾病多关注病因学，精神疾病多关注社会行为特征）。模型验证的宏观平均Cohen's Kappa得分为0.832，显示出良好的一致性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的NOMAD本体论成功填补了疾病命名规范化框架的空白。通过大规模分类分析，研究揭示了医学命名法不仅反映了疾病特征，还体现了不同学科的认识论传统和社会文化偏见（如命名中的性别不平等）。这为未来建立更加系统、透明的医学命名标准提供了重要的科学依据。

Abstract: The nomenclature of human disease has developed organically over the past centuries using Greek, Latin, and Arabic terminology and reflects the idiosyncrasies of different eras of medical discovery. Despite evident heterogeneity in naming practices, no systematic framework exists for characterising these conventions across all diseases. In this paper, we describe the Nomenclature Ontology for Medical And Disease names (NOMAD), a meta-taxonomy that classifies disease names according to their naming conventions. We developed a two-level taxonomy comprising 9 top-level categories and 20 subcategories and applied it to 22,548 index entries from the ICD-10-CM 2026 Alphabetical Index in a scalable three-stage machine learning-driven classification pipeline. Classification was multi-label, reflecting the compositional nature of medical nomenclature. We classified 99.1% of terms with a mean of 2.12 labels per entry. Anatomical categories were the most prevalent (63.8% of entries), followed by Descriptive (48.4%) and Pathophysiological (40.2%), while Eponymous and Geographical labels were less common than their cultural prominence might suggest (9.7% and 1.9% respectively). Among all Eponymous diseases, we identified only 57 (2.6%) of diseases named after a female person. We manually reviewed a random sample of n=2,255 entries (10%) for accuracy and calculated a full agreement rate of 70% and partial agreement rate of 26% (macro-averaged Cohen's Kappa score 0.832). Naming convention profiles varied substantially across ICD-10-CM chapters, reflecting specialty-specific epistemological traditions: infectious disease chapters were dominated by etiological labels and showed the highest proportion of geographical region related labels, the circulatory chapter by anatomical and pathophysiological labels, and mental and behavioural disorders showed the highest prevalence of socio-behavioral labels.

</details>


### [178] [TASR: Training-Free Adaptive Stopping for Iterative Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13814)
*Adrian Kieback,Uyiosa Philip Amadasun,Aman Chadha,Aaron Elkins*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: TASR 是一种无需训练的迭代 RAG 停止策略，通过监测答案重复和 Logit 边际来智能终止多余的检索调用，在大幅降低成本的同时保持了高效的预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 迭代检索增强生成（RAG）智能体在模型已获取足够信息并收敛后，往往会进行多余的检索，导致调用成本浪费且对预测性能无贡献。现有的基于学习的停止策略通常需要针对特定模型或任务进行重训练，缺乏通用性和便捷性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 TASR 的“无需训练自适应停止规则”。该方法由一个单行谓词定义：当模型在当前轮次输出的答案（归一化处理后）与上一轮一致，且经过等调校准的 Logit 边际超过 0.25 时，触发停止。该方法无需额外的分类器或价值头，且在不同模型、检索器和语料库配置下阈值固定。

Result: TASR 在 24 种配置下表现稳健。在 3 模型 x 2 数据集的干扰测试中，它以 62.6% 的调用量保留了固定 k=5 策略 94.8% 的 F1 分数，且性能超过了固定 k=3。在开放域 BM25 及稠密检索任务中，均实现了在减少调用次数的同时保持或提升准确率的效果。分析显示，Logit 边际相比 RLHF 微调模型的置信度分数具有更好的区分度。

Conclusion: TASR 提供了一种无需训练、可审计且具有帕累托最优性的停止规则。它证明了在迭代 RAG 中，利用归一化答案重复度和校准后的 Logit 边际可以有效识别模型收敛状态，显著降低不必要的检索成本，是未来学习型停止控制器的强有力基准。

Abstract: Iterative retrieval-augmented generation agents commonly overspend by continuing to retrieve after the model has converged on an answer, incurring calls that change neither the prediction nor the supporting evidence. Existing remedies learn a stopping policy from labeled trajectories, tying the decision to a trained component that requires retraining for each new model or task. We propose TASR (Training-Free Adaptive Stopping Rule), a one-line predicate that fires when the model repeats its previous-round normalized answer and the isotonically calibrated logit margin exceeds 0.25. No classifier or value head is learned; the threshold is fixed across all twenty-four (model, retriever, corpus) configurations we evaluate. On a 3-model x 2-dataset distractor grid, TASR retains 94.8% of fixed-k=5's macro F1 at 62.6% of its calls and exceeds fixed-k=3 by +3.42 F1. The pattern holds on nine open-domain BM25 cells (55.01 F1 at 2.98 calls vs. 54.33 at 3.00 for fixed-k=3) and, with calibration locked from the distractor split, on nine dense-retrieval cells across two retriever families, with zero significant regressions in either extension. The rule was selected from an exhaustive enumeration of 381 candidate stopping rules; no alternative Pareto-dominates it on any evaluated configuration. A signal-quality analysis shows that verbalized 1-5 confidence collapses on RLHF-tuned models (96.5% of values equal 5, entropy 0.182 nats), while the logit margin achieves 44x better class-conditional separation, grounding the design in a measurable model pathology. TASR is an auditable, training-free Pareto baseline against which learned stopping controllers can be compared. Code is publicly available.

</details>


### [179] [Hybrid Neural Retrieval with Generative Query Refinement for Quranic Passage Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13837)
*Mohamed G. Salman,Mohammad E. Moftah,Ali Hamdi*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对古兰经检索中语言语义鸿沟和多经文查询的难点，本文提出了一种四阶段神经架构，通过混合检索、语义重排序、信心过滤及多经文细化，显著提升了检索的准确性与上下文理解能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 古兰经经文检索（PR）面临现代标准阿拉伯语（MSA）与经典阿拉伯语（CA）之间的语言复杂性和语义鸿沟，导致传统检索方法效果不佳。此外，现有系统在处理多经文检索和零结果查询过滤方面存在局限。

Method: 提出了一种四阶段神经架构：1. 混合检索：结合AraColBERT（密集索引）与BM25（稀疏检索）；2. 语义重排序：使用CAMeLBERTmix交叉编码器；3. 信心门控机制：用于过滤无结果查询；4. 细化模块：基于AraT5进行多经文聚合。

Result: 在扩展后的Quran QA 2022数据集上，模型表现优于基准模型，Recall@10达到0.7024，MAP@10达到0.4947，MRR为0.5807。

Conclusion: 该研究通过集成多种深度学习技术，成功构建了一个针对古兰经语境的稳健检索框架。尽管在顶级精度上与单模型存在微小权衡，但该四阶段架构在处理复杂多经文查询和减少无结果查询方面表现出色，为古兰经信息检索提供了更全面、可靠的解决方案。

Abstract: Quranic Passage Retrieval (PR) could be a challenging task due to the linguistic complexity and the semantic gap between the Modern Standard Arabic (MSA) used in daily queries and the Classical Arabic (CA) of the Holy Quran. These factors hinder conventional retrieval methods. To handle these limitations and improve multi-verse retrieval and filter the zero-answer queries, this paper proposes a four-phase neural architecture designed to enhance retrieval accuracy and contextual understanding. The methodology combines hybrid candidate retrieval using AraColBERT dense indexing and BM25 sparse retrieval, followed by semantic reranking with a CAMeLBERTmix cross-encoder. A confidence gating mechanism is then applied to filter zero-answer queries, and an AraT5-based refinement module for multi-verse aggregation. The system is evaluated on an expanded version of the Quran QA 2022 dataset. Results show improved performance compared to the baseline models, achieving a Recall@10 of 0.7024 and a Mean Average Precision (MAP@10) of 0.4947. While the system exhibits a marginal tradeoff in absolute top-rank precision (MRR = 0.5807) compared to heavily optimised single models, the proposed architecture provides a substantially more comprehensive, reliable, and context aware solution for multi-verse Quranic passage retrieval.

### [180] [Mood-Aware Music Recommendation: Integrating User Affective Signals into Ranking Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13858)
*Terence Zeng,Abhishek K. Umrawal*

Main category: cs.IR

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统协同过滤在音乐推荐中常受限于交互数据的稀疏性，而现有的基于内容的推荐多关注流派或歌词等属性，忽略了用户情感状态对音乐选择的关键影响。因此，研究旨在利用情绪识别技术来优化个性化推荐体验。

Method: 提出了一种基于情绪（能量-效价空间）的条件化排序框架，通过Softmax采样技术将用户的情感信号有机地整合到推荐算法中，并采用单盲实验对该系统与基准模型进行了对比验证。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了将用户的情感状态作为个性化音乐推荐的重要维度是切实有效的，能够显著提升用户对推荐质量的主观感知。情绪感知的整合为解决传统协同过滤在音乐推荐领域中面临的稀疏性问题提供了新的思路。

Abstract: Recommendation systems are essential in modern music streaming platforms due to the vast amount of available content. While collaborative filtering is widely used to suggest items based on the preferences of others with similar patterns, it performs poorly in domains where user-item interactions are sparse, such as music. Content-based filtering is an alternative approach that examines the qualities of the items themselves. Genre, instrumentation, and lyrics have been explored; however, relatively little attention has been given to emotion recognition. Since a user's emotional state strongly influences their music choice, incorporating mood signals offers a promising direction for personalization. In this work, we propose a mood-conditioned ranking framework that integrates user affective signals into the recommendation process via softmax-based sampling in the energy-valence space. We evaluate the approach via single-blind experiments in which participants compare recommendations from the proposed system against a baseline. The results indicate improved perceived recommendation quality, providing preliminary evidence for the effectiveness of incorporating mood-based inputs into music recommendations.

### [181] [ADORE: Iterative Query Expansion with Retrieval-Grounded Relevance Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13905)
*Amin Bigdeli,Negar Arabzadeh,Radin Hamidi Rad,Sajad Ebrahimi,Charles L. A. Clarke,Ebrahim Bagheri*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对现有查询扩展方法容易导致检索漂移的问题，本文提出了ADORE框架。该框架引入检索反馈机制，通过迭代式观察检索结果并进行相关性评估，指导LLM进行更精准的查询扩展，显著提升了信息检索的准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于LLM的查询扩展方法大多仅依赖单次生成或未经验证的迭代，缺乏对目标语料库实际检索效果的考量。这种单纯的“生成式”思路容易导致检索漂移、放大误导性词汇或遗漏区分性术语，从而限制了检索效果。

Method: 提出ADORE（ADapt, Observe, Relevance Evaluate）框架，这是一种迭代式查询扩展方法。该方法包含三个关键步骤：1. 利用LLM生成伪段落；2. 通过检索器获取语料库的响应；3. 通过相关性评估器根据原始查询对检索结果进行判断，利用评估反馈指导下一次的查询扩展，从而实现对关键信息的强化和对噪音的抑制。

Result: 在TREC Deep Learning、BEIR和BRIGHT等数据集上，ADORE表现优异。在BEIR数据集上，其nDCG@10较BM25提升24.5%，较现有最强基线提升3.6%；在BRIGHT数据集上，较BM25提升122.9%，较最强基线提升9.2%。实验结果表明该方法在多种场景下均具有显著优势。

Conclusion: ADORE框架证明了将检索结果作为反馈循环纳入查询扩展过程的重要性。通过迭代式地观察、评估和调整，模型能够更有效地弥补检索偏差，实现比传统生成式查询扩展方法显著且更具鲁棒性的性能提升。

Abstract: LLM-based query expansion improves retrieval by enriching the original query with additional context. Yet most methods remain generation-driven, producing plausible pseudo-documents or expansions without checking how the target corpus responds. This can introduce retrieval drift, amplify misleading vocabulary, or miss terms that distinguish relevant from non-relevant documents. We argue that effective expansion requires retrieval-grounded feedback, not just single-pass generation or unverified iteration. We introduce ADORE (ADapt, Observe, Relevance Evaluate), an iterative framework that turns retrieval outcomes into feedback for the next expansion. At each round, an LLM generates pseudo-passages, a retriever exposes the corpus response, and a relevance assessor evaluates retrieved documents against the original query. These judgments identify what to reinforce, what remains undercovered, and what to suppress. Across TREC Deep Learning, BEIR, and BRIGHT, ADORE consistently outperforms strong query expansion baselines with notable improvements across nearly all evaluation settings, improving average nDCG@10 by 24.5% over BM25 and 3.6% over the strongest prior query expansion method on BEIR, and by 122.9% over BM25 and 9.2% over the best query expansion baseline on BRIGHT. Our code and data are publicly available.

</details>


### [182] [When Recommendation Denoising Meets Popularity Bias: Understanding and Mitigating Their Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14046)
*Guohang Zeng,Jie Lu,Guangquan Zhang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对推荐系统中小损失去噪策略导致的“误删”长尾正样本问题，提出流行度感知去噪（PAD），通过区分物品流行度来差异化处理噪声，有效缓解了长尾偏差并提升了整体推荐质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的去噪推荐方法多依赖于“小损失”启发式策略（即认为损失值小的样本是干净的），但忽略了流行度偏差。该策略会导致模型将难以拟合的真实长尾正样本误判为噪声，从而加剧推荐系统中的头部效应和长尾稀疏性问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为“流行度感知去噪”（PAD）的轻量级插件框架。该方法通过引入物品流行度信息来调节去噪强度：对高曝光的头部物品施加更强的去噪力度，而对长尾物品采取更保守的去噪策略，从而保留更多真实的稀疏长尾信号。

Result: 在三个数据集和三种模型架构上的实验表明，PAD方法优于现有的多种去噪基准模型，并在准确率（Accuracy）与多样性（Diversity）之间取得了更优的平衡，特别是在MF类推荐模型中表现尤为显著。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了传统的基于小损失启发式（small-loss heuristic）的去噪方法在面对长尾物品时存在严重的偏差，并提出了PAD框架以平衡噪声过滤与长尾信号保护。实验证明，该方法能有效提升推荐系统的准确性与多样性。

Abstract: Implicit feedback is the dominant data source for recommender systems, but behavioral logs are often contaminated by false-positive interactions caused by mis-clicks, biased exposure, and interface effects. Denoising recommendation methods improve robustness by down-weighting or filtering interactions suspected to be noisy, often relying on the small-loss heuristic. We revisit this heuristic through the lens of popularity bias. Tail-item positives can be harder to fit because they are sparsely observed, and thus may receive larger losses even when they reflect genuine user preference. Under such popularity-dependent loss patterns, monotone loss-based reweighting can suppress clean-but-hard tail signals and increase the head-tail imbalance in effective supervision.
  We formalize this interaction through the effective head-tail signal ratio induced by denoising weights and derive a conditional reallocation result: when the loss distribution of tail positives is right-shifted relative to that of head positives, small-loss reweighting increases the effective head-tail signal ratio compared with ERM. Motivated by this analysis, we propose Popularity-Aware Denoising (PAD), a lightweight plug-in framework that modulates denoising strength by item popularity. PAD applies stronger denoising to highly exposed items while being more conservative on tail items, preserving more clean-but-hard long-tail signals. Experiments on three datasets and three backbones show that PAD generally improves over representative denoising baselines and provides favorable accuracy-diversity tradeoffs, especially on MF-style recommenders.

</details>


### [183] [Knowledge Graph Enhanced Memory-Augmented Retrieval for Long Context Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14047)
*Ghadir Alselwi,Basem Suleiman,Hao Xue,Shoaib Jameel,Hakim Hacid,Flora D. Salim,Imran Razzak*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: KGERMAR 框架通过在长文本推理中实时构建动态知识图谱，融合结构化关系信息与文本语义，在提升模型性能的同时显著提高了内存效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的长文本语言模型主要依赖语义相似度，难以准确维护长序列中复杂的实体状态和关系。该研究旨在通过引入显式的结构化知识增强模型对上下文的理解能力。

Method: 提出了一种名为 KGERMAR 的框架，在推理阶段从输入文本中实时提取实体和关系以构建动态上下文知识图谱；采用包含上下文、语义和结构三个组件的多内存架构，并通过学习到的权重融合 retrieval 信号，将图结构嵌入与文本语义集成。

Result: 在多个数据集（SlimPajama, WikiText-103, PG-19, Proof-pile）上验证，KGERMAR 在 1K 到 32K Token 的上下文长度下，困惑度（Perplexity）降低了 8.5%，内存效率提升了 2-2.5 倍，并在五个 NLU 任务中表现出更强的上下文学习能力。

Conclusion: KGERMAR 通过引入动态构建的上下文知识图谱，成功解决了长文本建模中实体关系理解不足的问题，证明了将显式结构化知识与隐含语义特征相结合是提升长文本模型性能的有效途径。

Abstract: Long-context language modeling requires not only extending context windows but maintaining coherent understanding of entity states and relationships across thousands of tokens -- a challenge that semantic similarity alone cannot address. KGERMAR addresses this by constructing dynamic, context-specific knowledge graphs from input text during inference, enabling domain-adaptive retrieval that leverages both semantic similarity and explicit entity relationships. The framework performs real-time entity and relation extraction to build contextual knowledge graphs, then integrates graph-structural embeddings with textual semantics through a multi-component memory architecture. Three memory banks -- contextual, semantic, and structural -- are maintained with retrieval signals fused via learned weights to capture both surface-level semantics and deeper relational patterns. Evaluated on SlimPajama (84.7K training examples), WikiText-103 (4,358 examples), PG-19 (100 examples), and Proof-pile (46.3K examples), KGERMAR achieves up to 8.5\% lower perplexity and 2--2.5x better memory efficiency than memory-augmented baselines across context lengths from 1K to 32K tokens, with superior in-context learning performance across five NLU tasks. The dynamic knowledge graph construction approach advances memory-augmented language modeling by enabling domain-specific knowledge representation that adapts to input contexts rather than relying on fixed knowledge bases.

</details>


### [184] [CoRe: A Continuously Reward-Finetuned LLM Query Rewriter for Multi-Stage Context-Aware Relevance in Web-Scale Video Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14127)
*Yilin Wen,Rong Yang,Xiaojia Chang,Hong Sun,Gefu Tang,Chunhui Liu,Jeffrey Chen,Zeyu Ma,Lisong Qiu,Xiaochuan Fan,Congjia Yu,Quan Zhou,Yuheng Chen,Zian Wang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: CoRe 是一个用于生产环境的 LLM 查询重写系统，它通过直接利用生产环境的排序反馈作为奖励信号，并结合高效的半在线混合偏好优化（MPO）循环，实现了在低计算开销下的持续迭代与性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生产环境中的 LLM 查询重写器面临着训练奖励无法准确反映重写结果在排序器中表现的矛盾，同时面临数据漂移导致的频繁重训练开销问题。因此，需要一种既能精准映射生产环境反馈，又具备低计算成本、支持持续部署的优化系统。

Method: CoRe 提出了一种基于生产环境多模态相关性模型的奖励函数，采用与生产融合代数一致的乘法比率形式以缩小离线与在线间的差距。系统利用半在线混合偏好优化（Mixed Preference Optimization）循环，仅对采样轨迹的 top-k/bottom-k 子集进行 DPO 风格的梯度更新，并采用分阶段同步机制降低计算开销，同时引入自动化晋级门控机制监测奖励欺骗。

Result: 在大型短视频搜索引擎的长达五个月的生产环境部署中，CoRe 通过两次 A/B 测试验证了其有效性：显著降低了受重写影响查询的“更改查询率”（change-query rate），并使所有主要的相关性和用户参与度指标均表现出预期的正向提升。

Conclusion: CoRe 证明了将生产环境排序器的反馈直接整合到查询重写器的训练循环中是可行且有效的。通过半在线优化策略和自动化评估，该系统能够适应数据漂移，在保持系统稳定性的同时显著提升了搜索的相关性和用户参与度。

Abstract: LLM-based query rewriters in production face a tension: the training reward must reflect how the rewrite is consumed by the production ranker, yet the training procedure must be cheap enough to support continuous redeployment as data drifts. We present CoRe (Context Relevance), such a system, redeployed weekly for over five months in a major short-video search engine. Our reward uses the deployed multimodal relevance model as its source and a multiplicative ratio form mirroring the production fusion algebra, closing the simulation-production gap that offline reward proxies leave open. A semi-online Mixed Preference Optimization loop makes this reward affordable at multi-million-instance weekly scale: a DPO-style pairwise objective restricts the gradient pass to a small top-k/bottom-k subset of sampled trajectories, and a phase structure reduces trainer/inference-server parameter syncs from per-step to per-phase. An automated promotion gate over reward-like and stability metrics detected and recovered from a real reward-hacking incident in production. Rewriter output is consumed as parallel relevance signals at recall, rawrank, and finerank without displacing the original signals, bounding rewriter-failure blast radius. Online A/B from two sequential production launches, first deploying the rewriter at finerank, then extending consumption to recall and rawrank, delivers statistically significant reductions in change-query rate on rewrite-impacted queries, with all headline relevance and engagement metrics moving in the expected direction.

</details>


### [185] [ChronoID: Infusing Explicit Temporal Signals into Semantic IDs for Generative Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14260)
*Dongdong Nian,Dongqi Fu,Chenliang Xu,Yinglong Xia,Hong Li,Hong Yan,Jian Kang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了ChronoID框架，通过在生成式推荐的语义ID中显式引入时间维度，解决了现有模型忽略用户兴趣随时间动态演变的问题，提升了推荐的准确性与时效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的生成式推荐系统通常使用时间不可知的语义ID，这忽略了用户意图和物品语义随时间演变的动态特性，导致系统将不同时间上下文的交互混淆为相同的语义表示，无法准确捕捉用户不断变化的偏好。

Method: 作者提出了一个统一框架“ChronoID”，旨在实现时间感知的语义ID学习。该方法通过系统化定义时间信号的三个正交维度，探索了显式时间信息的注入方式，并构建了一个新的时间显式生成推荐基准，用于评估时间注入的有效性、架构设计及性能增益来源。

Result: 研究结果表明，通过ChronoID将时间信息显式注入语义ID可以有效缓解语义表示的时间平稳性假设偏差。实验证明了该方法在处理动态交互节奏时的优越性，并揭示了有效注入时间信息的关键架构设计策略。

Conclusion: 本文证明了将时间显式纳入语义ID对生成式推荐系统至关重要。通过ChronoID框架和新基准测试，研究表明时间感知语义ID能够有效捕捉用户兴趣的演变，克服了传统方法对时间不敏感的局限性，从而显著提升推荐效果。

Abstract: Semantic IDs are crucial in generative recommendation, but with a fundamental limitation: temporal information is not well incorporated into semantic IDs. Instead, time influences recommendation only implicitly (e.g., through session construction heuristics, preference alignment, or sequence order), while existing semantic ID learning remains entirely time-agnostic. This design conflates interactions occurring under distinct temporal contexts into identical semantic representations, implicitly assuming that item semantics and user intent are temporally stationary. Such an assumption is misaligned with real-world recommendation scenarios, where evolving interaction rhythms play a central role. In this work, we investigate where and how the explicit time should be incorporated into semantic ID for generative recommendation. First, we systematically characterize the design space along three orthogonal dimensions of temporal signals and present a unified framework, ChronoID, for time-aware semantic ID learning. Then, by contributing a new time-explicit generation recommendation benchmark, ChronoID answers the questions: what is the effective way of infusing time, how to design the architecture, and where does the gain come from.

</details>


### [186] [ScoreGate: Adaptive Chunk Selection for Retrieval-Augmented Generation via Dual-Score Statistical Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14269)
*Karamvir Singh,Arvind Jain*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: ScoreGate 是一种轻量级的自适应检索机制，通过利用双编码器和交叉编码器的评分信息动态确定检索块数量，在显著降低计算成本和 token 消耗的同时，保证了甚至提升了检索的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的固定 Top-K 检索策略无法适应查询复杂度的变化。对于简单查询，它会导致过度检索；对于复合查询，则可能导致检索不足（遗漏关键信息）。现有方法未能有效利用交叉编码器来纠正双编码器在词汇不匹配情况下的失效，因此需要一种能够自动控制检索规模的轻量级方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ScoreGate 的轻量级评分空间决策机制。该机制利用现有的双编码器（bi-encoder）相似度分数和交叉编码器（cross-encoder）重排序分数作为输入，无需额外的模型推理，即可在推理阶段动态决定每个查询所需检索的块数量，解决了固定 Top-K 带来的过度检索或检索不足问题。

Result: 在 MS MARCO 数据集上，ScoreGate 在减少 35% 检索块的情况下，MRR@10 达到 0.401；在内部基准测试中，保持了 97.77%-99.34% 的高召回率，每查询 token 数量减少 34.8%，且仅增加 31ms 延迟。

Conclusion: ScoreGate 通过自适应调整检索块数量，实现了在不降低检索质量的前提下，显著提升检索效率的目标，验证了动态检索基数在处理复杂查询时的优势。

Abstract: Fixed-cardinality retrieval injects a constant top-K chunks into the generator regardless of query complexity, causing over-retrieval for narrow queries and under-retrieval for compositional ones. We describe ScoreGate, a lightweight score-space decision mechanism that controls retrieval cardinality at inference time using two scores already produced by the standard pipeline: bi-encoder similarity s_i and cross-encoder reranker score r_i, with no additional model inference calls required. Its core insight is that cross-encoder affirmation can rescue semantically relevant chunks that bi-encoder retrieval ranks poorly due to vocabulary mismatch -- a failure mode unaddressed by fixed-K or single-score thresholding. On MS MARCO (200 dev queries), ScoreGate achieves MRR@10 = 0.401 with 35% fewer retained chunks than Standard Top-K. On an internal benchmark (n=300, Fleiss' kappa=0.87), ScoreGate observed zero false positives (95% CI [96.4%, 100%]) at 97.77-99.34% recall, with 34.8% fewer tokens per query and only 31ms added latency. Results on both MS MARCO and real-world production traffic suggest that adaptive retrieval cardinality can improve retrieval efficiency without degrading retrieval quality.

</details>


### [187] [Verifiable User Simulation for Search and Recommendation Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14474)
*Chenglong Ma,Xinye Wanyan,Danula Hettiachchi,Ziqi Xu,Yongli Ren,Jeffrey Chan*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一个针对基于LLM用户模拟器的设计与审计框架，旨在解决模拟器不透明及潜在的偏见问题，通过七个可审计组件确保模拟行为的可解释性、一致性与公平性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于大语言模型（LLM）的用户模拟器存在“黑盒”问题，难以解释模拟行为的动机及其与用户画像的一致性；此外，模拟器在面对不同文化、教育背景及语言群体时可能产生偏见或歧视，缺乏公平性保障。

Method: 提出了一套包含七个可审计组件的设计与审计框架：结构化角色（Persona）、任务感知契约（Contract）、人机匹配执行（Execution）、可审计追踪（Trace）、角色对齐验证（Verification）、结构化反馈（Feedback）及更新循环（Refinement）。通过“推荐列表评估”和“搜索查询构建”两个实践实验室进行教学。

Result: 为研究人员和从业者提供了一套切实可行的框架和评估工具，用于识别模拟器行为中的偏差，区分诊断差异分析与统计验证，并确保模拟器在搜索和推荐任务中的可靠性与公平性。

Conclusion: 本文通过提出一套系统的设计与审计框架，强调了在构建用户模拟器时，必须通过全流程的审计和验证机制来确保模拟器行为的可解释性、公平性和对用户画像的忠实度，以支持负责任的AI开发。

Abstract: Large-language-model (LLM) based user simulation is increasingly adopted for evaluating search engines, recommender systems, and retrieval-augmented generation pipelines, yet most simulators remain opaque: it is difficult to determine why a simulated user made a particular choice or whether that choice is consistent with the intended user profile. Compounding this, recent research shows that LLMs can produce biased or discriminatory responses depending on user background characteristics such as language, education level, and cultural context, raising concerns about the equitable treatment of minority and disadvantaged groups. This half-day, in-person tutorial introduces a proposed design-and-audit framework that treats a user simulator as a verifiable engineering artefact composed of seven auditable components - structured Persona, task-aware Contract, matched human-vs-agent Execution, auditable Trace, persona-aligned Verification, structured Feedback, and a Refinement loop that updates personas and contracts. Through two hands-on mini-labs on recommendation-list evaluation and search-query formulation, participants will inspect simulator behaviour end-to-end, distinguish diagnostic discrepancy analysis from statistical validation, and apply checks for fidelity, credibility, and demographic bias. The tutorial targets information retrieval and recommender systems researchers and practitioners interested in user behaviour simulation and responsible AI.

</details>


### [188] [Private Information Retrieval for Large-Scale DNA-Based Data Storage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14557)
*Gökberk Erdoğan,Daniella Bar-Lev,Rawad Bitar,Antonia Wachter-Zeh,Zohar Yakhini*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文探讨了如何在DNA数据存储中实现私有信息检索（PIR），针对生化查询的特殊性提出了两种双服务器协议，以平衡数据隐私、检索效率与生物实验的执行难度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DNA数据存储具有高密度和长久保存的潜力，但缺乏对数据隐私的有效保护。传统的PIR协议难以直接应用于DNA存储，因为生化检索机制具有特殊的复杂性和物理局限性，因此需要针对该领域开发专门的隐私保护方案。

Method: 研究针对双服务器架构，提出了两种适配DNA存储特性的私有信息检索（PIR）协议。这些方法通过优化生化查询过程的复杂性，将传统的数字域PIR逻辑转化为适合DNA物理存储环境的检索机制。

Result: 成功构建了适用于DNA存储环境的两种双服务器PIR协议，验证了在保障用户查询隐私的前提下，能够有效管理生化查询带来的复杂性，并揭示了不同协议在隐私保护程度、检索效率和生物实验可行性之间的权衡。

Conclusion: 本文表明，将信息论隐私保护机制引入DNA数据存储是可行且必要的。通过平衡隐私性、计算效率与生化可行性，研究为DNA存储系统的安全检索提供了理论框架和实践指导，展示了隐私与存储性能之间的权衡关系。

Abstract: We investigate Private Information Retrieval (PIR) in the context of synthetic DNA-based data storage. While PIR is a well-studied primitive for digital databases, extending it to DNA-based databases presents unique challenges arising from biochemical query mechanisms and their complexity. We propose two approaches for adapting two-server PIR protocols to DNA-based storage, balancing privacy, efficiency, and feasibility. These approaches illustrate how information-theoretic privacy trade-offs manifest in DNA-based storage systems.
